 pehle ye film republic de par aane vaali thi lekin pedman se klesh se bachane ke liye film ko 9 farvari se aage badhaakar 16 farvari kar diya gaya
 storythe story of the film begins with the notions of Colonel Abhay Singh (manoj Bajpai) and Major Jai Bakhshi (siddharth Malhotra)
 yah donon bhartiya army ke liye kaam karte hai lekin kuch aise vaakye hote hai jinaki vajah se jai achaanak se dilli se gaayab hone kii firaaq main lag jaataa he

 kuch ahm muddon par bade hi sulajhe tareeke se dhyaan khinchne kii koshish kii gai he

 loksabhaa chunaav 2019 main matdaan ke dauraan hinsak ghatnaon ke liye surkhiyon main aae pashchim bengal main agsit pole ke nattejey bijepi kaa khush karne vaale hai to tiemasi mukhiya mamata banerjee ko pareshaan karne vaale
 In the exit poll of the country's most trusted Aaj Tak- Axis My India, BJP got 19-23 seats out of 42 in the state
 vahiin mamata banerjee kii trinmul congress (TMC) ko 19-22 siten milti dikh raheen hai
 Thus, for the first time the BJP, which has been continuously increasing its base in West Bengal, has come in a state of shocking performance
 vah 2014 main mili do siton ke mukaable is baar 23 loksabhaa seat tak hasil karne kii haisiyat main dikh rahi he
 According to the exit poll, this time the account of the Left, which ruled for more than three decades in West Bengal, will not be opened
 pashchim bengal kii satta lambey arase tak congress or vam dal ke kabje main rahi
 In the 2011 assembly elections, the Trinamool Congress led by Mamata Banerjee overthrew the CPI-M, which had been ruling for 34 years
 raajnneetik vishleshak bataate hai ki congress ke kamjor hone or left ke ummiido par khara na utarane ke baad se yahaan kii janata ko ek majboot vipaksh kii bhi jarurat mahasoos hui to ye sambhaavnaaen unhen bijepi main dikhi
 This is the reason that the vote percentage of BJP gradually increased and now BJP has become the number two party in the state
 is baar pashchim bengal kii zyaadaatar siton par tiemasi, bijepi or congress ke bich trikoniya ladaai kii sambhaavna rahi he
 But exit poll figures show that the fight in the state was reduced to one between TMC and BJP
 chunavi reliyon main bhi mamata or modi ek duusare par hi jubaani hamalaa bolne main zyada vakt kharch karte najar aae
 This made this election of Dada vs Didi
 2014 or 2016 main mamata kii party kaa pradarshan2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav main mamata banerjee kii trinmul congress(tmc) ko 42 main se 34 siten milin thim, jabaki bijepi ko sirf do siten, vahiin congress ko chaar or vammorcha ko do loksabhaa siten milin thim
 In this election, Mamata Banerjee's party got 40 percent vote share, while BJP got 17, Congress 10 and the Left Front got 25 percent vote share
 2016 ke vidhansabha chunaav kii baat karen to mamata banerjee ko kul 294 main 211 siten milin thim
 At the same time, Congress was second with 44 seats

 But the rest of the people in the Parliament House still did not know what happened or what was happening
 goliyon kii aawaaj ko zyaadaatar log pataakhon kaa shor samaj rahe the
 No one even thought that in the Parliament, even inside the Parliament House, terrorists can shout
 par phir tabhi goliyon kii tadatadaahat ke bich ek dhamaake kii aawaaj aati he
 After the echo of the bullets, the first blast had announced that the temple of the world's largest democracy, the Parliament House, has been attacked
 goliyon kii tadatadaahat or dhamaakon kii gunj ke bich surakshakarmiyon ko lahuluhaan jameen par girte dekh pal bhar main tasviir saaf ho chuki thi
 And now there was panic and panic all around inside the Parliament House
 jise jidhar jo konaa dikhaai de rahaa tha wo udhar hi bhaag rahaa tha
 Even now the loudest sound of gunfire was coming from the gate number 11
 paanchon aatankwaadi ab bhi ambesder car ke hi aas-paas se goliyaan or grenade barasaa rahe the
 Then, seeing the terrorists gathered towards gate number 11, the security personnel of Parliament House along with the Delhi Police and CRPF personnel move towards gate number 11
 ab donon taraf se golibari shuru ho chuki thi
 Home minister LK Advani, who was just a few hundred meters away from the firing, had also received news of the attack by then
 lihaaja, laalkrishna adwani or raksha mantri jorge furnandis samet tamaam varisht mantriyon ko fouran sadan ke andar hi mahfuj jagahon par le jaaya gaya
 With this, all the doors leading to the house are also closed and security personnel take their positions there
 udhar duusari taraf surakshakarmiyon ko get number 11 kii taraf badhate dekh paanchon aatankwaadi bhi apni pojishan badalane lagate hai
 One of the five terrorists now firing towards GATE No
 1 runs
 jabaki baaki chaar get number 12 kii taraf badhane kii koshish karte hai

 magar suraksha karmiyon ne pehle hi tamaam daravaajon ke ird-gird apni pojishan le rakhi thi

1
 vahiin se goliyaan barsaata hua sadan ke andar jane ke liye sansad bhawan ke galiyare se hote hue ek daravaaje kii taraf badhata he
 But before he succeeds in his attempt, he is shot by security forces
 goli lagate hi get number ek ke kareeb galiyare main hi daravaaje se kuch dur wo gir padataa he
 The first terrorist had fallen, but he was still alive
 surakshakarmi use puri tarah se nishane par lene ke baavjood uske kareeb jane se abhi bhi batch rahe the
 Because the fear was that he might blow himself away
 or surakshakarmiyon kaa ye dar galat bhi nahin tha
 Because immediately after falling on the ground, when the terrorist felt that he was surrounded, he immediately pressed himself on the remote and blew himself up
 usne apane sharir par bam baandh rakhaa tha
 Four terrorists were still alive
 na sirf jinda the balki lagaataar bhaag-bhaag kar andhadhundh goliyaan barasaa rahe the
 It was as if they had come prepared to compete for hours
 kyonki unke paas goli, bam or grenade kaa puraa jakhira tha
 Which he had hidden in his body and brought in a shoulder bag
 ab tak enesji commando or sena ko bhi hamale kii khabar di ja chuki thi
 The team of Special Cell of Delhi Police, which specializes in dealing with terrorists, had also traveled to Parliament House
 par sansad bhawan main live oparation ab bhi jari tha
 The news of the attack through the news channel had now spread to India and abroad
 is bich shaayad baaki bache chaar aatankwaadiyon ko bhi apane ek saathi kii maut kii khabar lag chuki thi
 Perhaps he got this news from a blast that was carried out by a terrorist by remotely blowing himself up
 lihaaja baaki aatankwaadi ab or zyada ghabara gaye
 In panic, all the four terrorists started running here and there to find the hideout
 duusari taraf surakshakarmi ab chaaron taraf se aatankwaadiyon ko gherna shuru kar chuke the
 The firing was still on
 or phir isi dauraan get number paanch se ek or acchhee khabar ai
 Another terrorist was pelted with security personnel's bullets
 ab bache teen aatankwaadi
 All three knew very well that they could not escape from the Parliament House alive
 lihaaza unhone bhi sadan ke andar jane kii ek aakhri koshish kii
 They started slowly moving towards Gate No
 9, firing the bullets
 magar mustaid surakshakarmiyon ne unhen get number nau ke paas hi gher liya

 There were continuous firing from both sides
 bich-bich main aatankwaadi surakshakarmiyon par hathgole bhi phenk rahe the
 But since they were surrounded all around, there was no way to escape now
 or aakhirkaar kuch der baad ek-ek kar teenon aatankwaadi dher ho chuke the

 Sultan Azlan Shah, the father of Malaysian hockey, died here today at the age of 86, which is considered a major loss for the international hockey
 sultan ajalan shah perek ke sultan the or unhen malaysian hockey kaa janak kaha jaataa tha
 He served the sport for 41 years as a player and administrator
 sultan ajalan shah ne yahaan aaj dopaher baad ek bajkar 30 minute par neshnal hart institute main antim saans lee
 His body will be taken to the Kuala Kangsar Palace and buried in the Royal Mausoleum in the afternoon
 sultan ajalan shah khel premi the or unhen hockey se vishesh lagaav tha
 This was the reason why he started the Sultan Azlan Shah Cup hockey tournament in 1983
 yah toornament pehle prayek do saal main yojit kiya jaataa tha, lekin 1998 ke baad iskaa har varsh aayojan kiya jane laga
 It is hosted by Ipoh, the capital of Perek
 apane schuli dinon main hockey khilne vaale sultan ajalan shah baad main perek kii taraf se bhi khele

 unki aguwai main malaysia ne 1975 ore 2002 main vishwa cap hockey kaa aayojan kiya
